Hafi y'imipfunda itatu y'ubukoloni bw'i Burayi (ubwa mbere muri Amerika, iya kabiri muri Aziya ndetse no muri Afurika nyuma), kugena ibidukikije byakoreshejwe mu gushyira mu byiciro abasangwabutaka mu nzego zishingiye ku moko.
Abayoborwa ninama rusange ninama zububasha ninama nkuru nayo iterana buri myaka ine.
Mu mwaka wa 2014, abahanga mu bukungu n’ikigo cy’ibipimo ngenderwaho cya Standard & Poor banzuye ko ubusumbane bwagutse hagati y’abenegihugu bakize bo muri Amerika ndetse n’abandi baturage bose bwatinze gukira kuva mu bukungu bwa 2008-2009 bityo bigatuma bikunda kwiyongera. inzinguzingu.
Iyubakwa rya "Official" naryo ryashyizwe ahagaragara na BBC kuri VHS, kuri MP3 CD-ROM, kandi nkibintu bidasanzwe kuri DVD.
Iki kibaya kigizwe na kilometero kare 7.000.000 (2.700.000 sq mi), muri zo kilometero kare 5.500.000 (kilometero kare 100.000) zuzuyeho amashyamba yimvura.
Bisaba umunyeshuri kuguma mwishuri mugihe runaka kumunsi wishuri (nka sasita, ikiruhuko cyangwa nyuma yishuri); cyangwa no kwitabira ishuri kumunsi utari ishuri, "Gufunga kwa gatandatu" byabereye mu mashuri amwe.
Mu 1709–13, icyorezo cy'icyorezo cyakurikiye Intambara ikomeye y'Amajyaruguru (1700-21, Suwede yaburanye n'Uburusiya n'abafatanyabikorwa) cyahitanye abagera ku 100.000 muri Suwede, na 300.000 muri Prussia.
